# Debt Protocol · Chapter 14 · Side Effect Sunrise

**File:** `media/novel/ch14-pNN.png` (match `NN` to panel id, e.g. `novel-p12` → `ch14-p12.png`).

## How to use these prompts
1. Copy the **Full prompt** for one panel into your image model as the **scene + art direction** positive (action, environment, lighting intent, readability, and framing).
2. Add **rendering medium and look** yourself—brush style, film grain, painterly vs clean line, palette, and any extra “no text” reinforcement—in a preset or a second positive block.
3. Match aspect ratio to **Layout** (wide splash vs tall tier).
4. Keep speech balloons off the render if you composite them in post; the site supplies balloon text separately.

---

## novel-p1 · page 1 · span-12

**Layout:** wide splash (~2:1 landscape). One strong establishing image; leave lower third relatively open for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

```
Morning in Sector 7 didn’t arrive with sun.
```

**Full prompt (paste into generator as one block):**

Comic book panel: Morning in Sector 7 didn’t arrive with sun. Cramped sci-fi interior: worn metal, cable runs, cold vapor, harsh practical lights. Art direction: grounded near-future sci-fi production design; clear focal hierarchy and readable silhouettes; directional practical light with motivated shadows; believable wear on materials; leave calm negative space where dialogue balloons composite in post; do not letter speech or captions inside the frame. Wide cinematic composition, landscape, strong environment read.

**Tracking (for filenames / sheets, not part of the image prompt):**

Chapter 14, Side Effect Sunrise, panel 1, comic page 1

## novel-p24 · page 12 · span-4 · UI readout

**Layout:** vertical tier panel (~4:5 portrait). Tight readable focal; leave margin for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

```
[PUBLICATION EVENT]
artifact: SIDE_EFFECT_MATRIX (public caches)
status: ACKNOWLEDGED
countermeasures: PENDING
public verification: RETAINED
note: interest accrual unaffected
```

**Full prompt (paste into generator as one block):**

Comic book panel: [PUBLICATION EVENT] artifact: SIDE_EFFECT_MATRIX (public caches) status: ACKNOWLEDGED countermeasures: PENDING public verification: RETAINED note: interest accrual unaffected Holographic HUD overlay: simple lines and symbols, abstract data shapes, not a wall of tiny readable text. Art direction: grounded near-future sci-fi production design; clear focal hierarchy and readable silhouettes; directional practical light with motivated shadows; believable wear on materials; leave calm negative space where dialogue balloons composite in post; do not letter speech or captions inside the frame. Screen glow and HUD readouts stay abstract—no micro-legible text blocks. Vertical comic panel, portrait emphasis, figure and set readable at a glance.

**Tracking (for filenames / sheets, not part of the image prompt):**

## novel-p33 · page 16 · span-6 · UI readout

**Layout:** vertical tier panel (~4:5 portrait). Tight readable focal; leave margin for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

```
[LEGAL ROUTER]
rider publication clause: SATISFIED (matrix)
executive response packet: FILED
classification: REMEDIATION / NARRATIVE HYGIENE
```
